Overview\n\nThis migration guide covers upgrading the Envoy External Processing HTTP filter from **v1.30.0 (April 2024)** to **v1.31.0 (July 2024)**. While this is a minor version update, it introduces important new features and refactors the route cache clearing mechanism.\n\n### Key Changes Summary\n\n| Category | Count | Impact |\n|----------|-------|--------|\n| Breaking Changes | 0 (strict) | Low |\n| Deprecated Fields | 1 | Medium |\n| New Features | 3 | Medium |\n| Behavioral Changes | 2 | Medium |\n\n---\n\n## 2. Breaking Changes\n\n### 2.1 No Strict Breaking Changes\n\n**Status:** ✅ Configurations from v1.30 will continue to work in v1.31\n\nThe ext_proc filter maintains backward compatibility - all v1.30 configurations will load and function in v1.31. However, there are important behavioral changes and deprecated fields that warrant attention.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Deprecated Features\n\n### 3.1 `disable_clear_route_cache` Field Deprecation\n\n**Deprecated Field:** `disable_clear_route_cache` (field 11)\n**Replacement:** `route_cache_action` (field 18)\n**Status:** Will be marked for removal in a future version\n**Motivation:** Provides more granular control over route cache behavior beyond simple enable/disable\n\n#### Details\n\nThe `disable_clear_route_cache` boolean field is now superseded by the more flexible `route_cache_action` enum. While the old field continues to work, the new field offers three distinct behaviors:\n\n**Proto Definition Change:**\n\n**v1.30.0:**\n```protobuf\n// api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto\n\nmessage ExternalProcessor {\n  // ...\n\n  // Prevents clearing the route-cache when the\n  // clear_route_cache field is set in an external processor response.\n  bool disable_clear_route_cache = 11;\n}\n```\n\n**v1.31.0:**\n```protobuf\n// api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto\n\nmessage ExternalProcessor {\n  enum RouteCacheAction {\n    // The default behavior is to clear the route cache only when the\n    // clear_route_cache field is set in an external processor response.\n    DEFAULT = 0;\n\n    // Always clear the route cache irrespective of the clear_route_cache bit in\n    // the external processor response.\n    CLEAR = 1;\n\n    // Do not clear the route cache irrespective of the clear_route_cache bit in\n    // the external processor response. Setting to RETAIN is equivalent to set the\n    // disable_clear_route_cache to true.\n    RETAIN = 2;\n  }\n\n  // Prevents clearing the route-cache when the\n  // clear_route_cache field is set in an external processor response.\n  // Only one of ``disable_clear_route_cache`` or ``route_cache_action`` can be set.\n  // It is recommended to set ``route_cache_action`` which supersedes ``disable_clear_route_cache``.\n  bool disable_clear_route_cache = 11\n      [(udpa.annotations.field_migrate).oneof_promotion = \"clear_route_cache_type\"];\n\n  // Specifies the action to be taken when an external processor response is\n  // received in response to request headers. It is recommended to set this field than set\n  // disable_clear_route_cache.\n  // Only one of ``disable_clear_route_cache`` or ``route_cache_action`` can be set.\n  RouteCacheAction route_cache_action = 18\n      [(udpa.annotations.field_migrate).oneof_promotion = \"clear_route_cache_type\"];\n}\n```\n\n#### Migration Steps\n\n**Option 1: Using `disable_clear_route_cache` (Current v1.30 Config)**\n```yaml\n# v1.30.0 configuration\nadmin:\n  address:\n    socket_address:\n      address: 127.0.0.1\n      port_value: 9901\n\nstatic_resources:\n  listeners:\n  - name: listener_0\n    address:\n      socket_address:\n        address: 0.0.0.0\n        port_value: 10000\n    filter_chains:\n    - filters:\n      - name: envoy.filters.network.http_connection_manager\n        typed_config:\n          \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.network.http_connection_manager.v3.HttpConnectionManager\n          stat_prefix: ingress_http\n          http_filters:\n          - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n            typed_config:\n              \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n              grpc_service:\n                envoy_grpc:\n                  cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n              disable_clear_route_cache: true  # ⚠️ DEPRECATED in v1.31.0\n              processing_mode:\n                request_header_mode: SEND\n                response_header_mode: SEND\n```\n\n**Option 2: Using `route_cache_action` (Recommended v1.31.0 Config)**\n```yaml\n# v1.31.0 configuration - RECOMMENDED\nadmin:\n  address:\n    socket_address:\n      address: 127.0.0.1\n      port_value: 9901\n\nstatic_resources:\n  listeners:\n  - name: listener_0\n    address:\n      socket_address:\n        address: 0.0.0.0\n        port_value: 10000\n    filter_chains:\n    - filters:\n      - name: envoy.filters.network.http_connection_manager\n        typed_config:\n          \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.network.http_connection_manager.v3.HttpConnectionManager\n          stat_prefix: ingress_http\n          http_filters:\n          - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n            typed_config:\n              \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n              grpc_service:\n                envoy_grpc:\n                  cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n              route_cache_action: RETAIN  # ✅ RECOMMENDED in v1.31.0\n              processing_mode:\n                request_header_mode: SEND\n                response_header_mode: SEND\n```\n\n#### Mapping Table\n\n| v1.30.0 Config | v1.31.0 Equivalent | Behavior |\n|----------------|-------------------|----------|\n| `disable_clear_route_cache: false` (default) | `route_cache_action: DEFAULT` | Clear cache only when ext_proc response requests it |\n| `disable_clear_route_cache: true` | `route_cache_action: RETAIN` | Never clear cache, regardless of ext_proc response |\n| — | `route_cache_action: CLEAR` | Always clear cache, regardless of ext_proc response |\n\n#### Validation Error\n\nIn v1.31.0, attempting to set both `disable_clear_route_cache` and `route_cache_action` to non-default values will result in a validation error:\n\n```\nEnvoyException: disable_clear_route_cache and route_cache_action can not be set to none-default at the same time.\n```\n\n**Implementation Reference:**\n`source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc:213-221`\n\n---\n\n## 4. New Features\n\n### 4.1 Observability Mode\n\n**Field:** `observability_mode` (field 17)\n**Type:** `bool`\n**Default:** `false`\n**Availability:** v1.31.0+\n**Status:** ✅ Fully Implemented\n\n#### Purpose\n\nObservability mode enables a \"send and go\" pattern where the ext_proc filter sends HTTP request/response data to the external processor **without waiting for responses**. This allows external processors to observe and analyze traffic without blocking the HTTP stream processing.\n\n#### Key Characteristics\n\n1. **Non-blocking:** Requests are sent asynchronously; responses are ignored\n2. **Streaming only:** Body processing mode is restricted to STREAMED or NONE\n3. **Stream closure:** External processor can close the stream to stop receiving data\n4. **No flow control:** Currently relies on external processor to handle backpressure\n5. **Deferred closure:** Streams are closed after a configurable timeout to prevent resource leaks\n\n#### Use Cases\n\n- **Monitoring and analytics:** Track all traffic patterns without affecting request processing\n- **Real-time logging:** Send detailed request/response information for downstream analysis\n- **Threat detection:** Analyze traffic for security anomalies without latency impact\n- **Compliance auditing:** Record all traffic for compliance requirements\n\n#### Configuration Example\n\n```yaml\nstatic_resources:\n  listeners:\n  - name: listener_0\n    address:\n      socket_address:\n        address: 0.0.0.0\n        port_value: 10000\n    filter_chains:\n    - filters:\n      - name: envoy.filters.network.http_connection_manager\n        typed_config:\n          \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.network.http_connection_manager.v3.HttpConnectionManager\n          stat_prefix: ingress_http\n          http_filters:\n          - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n            typed_config:\n              \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n              grpc_service:\n                envoy_grpc:\n                  cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n              observability_mode: true  # ✅ NEW in v1.31.0\n              processing_mode:\n                request_header_mode: SEND\n                response_header_mode: SEND\n                request_body_mode: STREAMED   # Only STREAMED or NONE allowed\n                response_body_mode: STREAMED  # Only STREAMED or NONE allowed\n              deferred_close_timeout: 5s  # Optional: timeout for stream closure\n```\n\n#### Behavioral Differences\n\n| Aspect | Normal Mode | Observability Mode |\n|--------|------------|-------------------|\n| Response Handling | Blocks processing, waits for response | Ignores responses |\n| Message Timeout | Enforced | Not enforced |\n| Body Modes | NONE, STREAMED, BUFFERED, BUFFERED_PARTIAL | STREAMED or NONE |\n| Stream Closure | Automatic | Deferred (configurable timeout) |\n| Use Case | Active modification/rejection | Passive observation |\n| Performance Impact | Adds latency | Minimal (fire-and-forget) |\n\n#### Implementation Details\n\n- **Header File:** `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.h:212`\n- **Implementation:** `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc:186, 405-408`\n- **New Methods:**\n  - `sendHeadersInObservabilityMode()` - sends headers without waiting\n  - `sendDataInObservabilityMode()` - sends body data without waiting\n  - `deferredCloseStream()` - closes stream after timeout\n\n### 4.2 Route Cache Action Enum\n\n**Field:** `route_cache_action` (field 18)\n**Type:** `enum RouteCacheAction`\n**Default:** `DEFAULT`\n**Availability:** v1.31.0+\n**Status:** ✅ Fully Implemented\n\n#### Purpose\n\nProvides explicit control over Envoy's route cache behavior when receiving responses from the external processor. This is more flexible than the boolean `disable_clear_route_cache` field.\n\n#### Enum Values\n\n```protobuf\nenum RouteCacheAction {\n  // The default behavior is to clear the route cache only when the\n  // clear_route_cache field is set in an external processor response.\n  DEFAULT = 0;\n\n  // Always clear the route cache irrespective of the clear_route_cache bit in\n  // the external processor response.\n  CLEAR = 1;\n\n  // Do not clear the route cache irrespective of the clear_route_cache bit in\n  // the external processor response.\n  RETAIN = 2;\n}\n```\n\n#### Decision Matrix\n\n| Scenario | DEFAULT | CLEAR | RETAIN |\n|----------|---------|-------|--------|\n| Ext_proc sets `clear_route_cache: true` | Cache cleared | Cache cleared | Cache NOT cleared |\n| Ext_proc sets `clear_route_cache: false` | Cache NOT cleared | Cache cleared | Cache NOT cleared |\n| Ext_proc doesn't set field | Cache NOT cleared | Cache cleared | Cache NOT cleared |\n\n#### Configuration Examples\n\n**Scenario 1: External processor controls cache clearing (DEFAULT)**\n```yaml\nroute_cache_action: DEFAULT  # Respect ext_proc decisions\n```\n\n**Scenario 2: Always refresh route on header modification (CLEAR)**\n```yaml\nroute_cache_action: CLEAR  # Always clear to ensure fresh routing decision\n# Use when external processor might modify request headers that affect routing\n```\n\n**Scenario 3: Never clear cache (RETAIN)**\n```yaml\nroute_cache_action: RETAIN  # Never clear, improve performance\n# Use when external processor only modifies non-routing headers\n```\n\n#### Implementation Reference\n\n- **Proto Definition:** `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto:105-120`\n- **Header File:** `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.h:232-235`\n- **Implementation:** `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc:187`\n\n### 4.3 Deferred Close Timeout\n\n**Field:** `deferred_close_timeout` (field 19)\n**Type:** `google.protobuf.Duration`\n**Default:** `5000ms` (5 seconds)\n**Availability:** v1.31.0+\n**Status:** ✅ Fully Implemented\n**Prerequisites:** Only applies when `observability_mode: true`\n\n#### Purpose\n\nControls how long gRPC streams to the external processor remain open in observability mode. This prevents streams from being held indefinitely while still allowing the external processor time to process outstanding messages.\n\n#### Configuration Example\n\n```yaml\nstatic_resources:\n  listeners:\n  - name: listener_0\n    address:\n      socket_address:\n        address: 0.0.0.0\n        port_value: 10000\n    filter_chains:\n    - filters:\n      - name: envoy.filters.network.http_connection_manager\n        typed_config:\n          \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.network.http_connection_manager.v3.HttpConnectionManager\n          stat_prefix: ingress_http\n          http_filters:\n          - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n            typed_config:\n              \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n              grpc_service:\n                envoy_grpc:\n                  cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n              observability_mode: true\n              processing_mode:\n                request_header_mode: SEND\n                response_header_mode: SEND\n              deferred_close_timeout: 10s  # Wait up to 10 seconds before closing stream\n```\n\n#### Default Behavior\n\nIf not specified, Envoy uses **5 seconds** (defined in code as `DEFAULT_DEFERRED_CLOSE_TIMEOUT_MS`).\n\n#### Tuning Recommendations\n\n| Scenario | Recommended Timeout | Reason |\n|----------|-------------------|--------|\n| Low-latency observation | 2-3s | Minimize resource usage |\n| Standard observation | 5s (default) | Balanced approach |\n| High-volume streaming | 10-15s | Allow time for processing bursts |\n| Batch processing | 30s+ | External processor batches and processes offline |\n\n#### Implementation Details\n\n- **Constant:** `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.h:150`\n- **Initialization:** `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc:188-189, 212-223`\n- **Stream Management:** `ThreadLocalStreamManager`, `DeferredDeletableStream` classes\n\n---\n\n## 5. Migration Steps\n\n### 5.1 Pre-Migration Checklist\n\n- [ ] Review current ext_proc configuration for deprecated fields\n- [ ] Audit external processor implementations for compatibility\n- [ ] Plan testing strategy for new features\n- [ ] Review metrics and logging for troubleshooting\n- [ ] Prepare rollback plan\n\n### 5.2 Step-by-Step Migration\n\n#### Step 1: Update Envoy Binary\n\n```bash\n# Backup current version\ncp /path/to/envoy /path/to/envoy-v1.30.bak\n\n# Install v1.31.0\n# Download or build Envoy v1.31.0\n# Verify binary: ./envoy --version\n```\n\n#### Step 2: Update Configuration Files\n\n**If using `disable_clear_route_cache`:**\n\n```bash\n# Find all configurations using the deprecated field\ngrep -r \"disable_clear_route_cache\" /etc/envoy/\n\n# Update each configuration\n# OLD:\n# disable_clear_route_cache: true\n\n# NEW:\n# route_cache_action: RETAIN\n```\n\n**Example migration script:**\n```bash\n#!/bin/bash\nfind /etc/envoy -name \"*.yaml\" -type f | while read file; do\n  if grep -q \"disable_clear_route_cache: true\" \"$file\"; then\n    sed -i 's/disable_clear_route_cache: true/route_cache_action: RETAIN/g' \"$file\"\n    echo \"Updated: $file\"\n  fi\ndone\n```\n\n#### Step 3: Validate Configuration\n\n```bash\n# Verify configuration syntax\n./envoy -c /etc/envoy/envoy.yaml --mode validate\n\n# Expected output:\n# configuration OK\n```\n\n#### Step 4: Test with Canary Deployment\n\n```bash\n# Deploy to canary environment with v1.31.0\n# Run integration tests\n# Monitor metrics:\n#   - ext_proc.streams_started\n#   - ext_proc.stream_msgs_sent\n#   - ext_proc.stream_msgs_received\n#   - ext_proc.message_timeouts\n#   - ext_proc.clear_route_cache_*\n```\n\n#### Step 5: Evaluate New Features\n\n**If interested in observability mode:**\n\n1. Deploy experimental configuration with `observability_mode: true`\n2. Monitor external processor resource usage\n3. Verify message delivery and stream closure behavior\n4. Adjust `deferred_close_timeout` based on observations\n\n#### Step 6: Production Rollout\n\n```bash\n# Rolling update strategy\n# 1. Update control plane configuration\n# 2. Rolling restart of Envoy instances (e.g., 25% at a time)\n# 3. Monitor for errors and performance changes\n# 4. Complete rollout when no issues detected\n```\n\n### 5.3 Validation Checklist\n\nAfter upgrading to v1.31.0:\n\n- [ ] Configuration loads without errors\n- [ ] No validation errors for ext_proc filter\n- [ ] External processor gRPC connectivity established\n- [ ] Metrics show normal request flow\n- [ ] No unexpected error rates\n- [ ] Route cache clearing behavior as expected\n- [ ] (If using observability_mode) Streams open/close normally\n\n---\n\n## 6. Behavioral Changes\n\n### 6.1 External Processor Timeout Response Code\n\n**Change:** Timeout handling now returns `504 Gateway Timeout`\n**Status:** ✅ Implemented in v1.31.0\n**Scope:** Applies when external processor doesn't respond within `message_timeout`\n\n#### Impact\n\n**v1.30.0 Behavior:**\n- Timeout errors might result in `500 Internal Server Error` or stream reset\n- Inconsistent behavior depending on filter state\n\n**v1.31.0 Behavior:**\n- Timeout errors consistently return `504 Gateway Timeout` to downstream client\n- More semantically correct (indicates upstream, not proxy)\n- Easier to identify external processor issues in metrics\n\n#### Example\n\n```\nClient Request → Envoy → Ext_proc Timeout\n↓\nEnvoy returns: 504 Gateway Timeout\nReason: External processor did not respond within message_timeout\n```\n\n### 6.2 Route Cache Action Default Behavior\n\n**Change:** Replaces implicit behavior with explicit enum\n**Status:** ✅ Implemented in v1.31.0\n**Scope:** Route cache clearing decision-making\n\n#### Impact\n\n**v1.30.0:**\n- Boolean flag (`disable_clear_route_cache: true/false`)\n- Limited to two states\n\n**v1.31.0:**\n- Enum with three explicit states\n- More expressive control over caching behavior\n- Better performance optimization possibilities\n\n---\n\n## 7. Testing Recommendations\n\n### 8.1 Unit Testing\n\n```bash\n# Run ext_proc filter unit tests\nbazel test //test/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc:...\n\n# Verify specific test categories\nbazel test //test/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc:ext_proc_filter_test\nbazel test //test/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc:ext_proc_integration_test\n```\n\n### 8.2 Integration Testing Strategy\n\n#### Test Case 1: Basic Functionality\n```\nObjective: Verify ext_proc filter processes headers correctly\nSteps:\n  1. Send HTTP request with custom headers\n  2. External processor modifies headers\n  3. Verify downstream receives modified headers\n  4. Verify response headers processed correctly\nExpected: All headers modified as expected, no errors\n```\n\n#### Test Case 2: Route Cache Action Behavior\n```\nObjective: Verify route_cache_action enum works correctly\nSteps:\n  1. Configure route_cache_action: DEFAULT\n  2. Modify request headers that affect routing\n  3. Verify route is re-evaluated (cache cleared)\n  4. Repeat with route_cache_action: RETAIN\n  5. Verify old route is still used (cache not cleared)\nExpected: Route caching behavior matches configuration\n```\n\n#### Test Case 3: Observability Mode\n```\nObjective: Verify observability_mode sends data without blocking\nSteps:\n  1. Enable observability_mode: true\n  2. Configure external processor to be slow (5s response time)\n  3. Send HTTP requests\n  4. Verify requests complete within normal time (not blocked)\n  5. Verify external processor eventually receives data\nExpected: Requests complete quickly, external processor receives data asynchronously\n```\n\n#### Test Case 4: Deferred Close Timeout\n```\nObjective: Verify deferred_close_timeout controls stream closure\nSteps:\n  1. Enable observability_mode: true\n  2. Set deferred_close_timeout: 2s\n  3. Send HTTP request\n  4. Monitor gRPC stream lifecycle\n  5. Verify stream closes approximately after 2 seconds\nExpected: Stream closes after configured timeout\n```\n\n#### Test Case 5: Timeout Handling\n```\nObjective: Verify external processor timeouts return 504\nSteps:\n  1. Configure external processor with slow response\n  2. Set message_timeout: 100ms\n  3. Send HTTP request\n  4. Verify response code is 504 Gateway Timeout\nExpected: 504 Gateway Timeout returned on timeout\n```\n\n### 8.3 Metrics Verification\n\nMonitor these metrics during testing:\n\n```bash\n# Count of streams started\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_streams_started\n\n# Count of messages sent to external processor\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_stream_msgs_sent\n\n# Count of messages received from external processor\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_stream_msgs_received\n\n# Count of message timeouts\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_message_timeouts\n\n# Count of clear_route_cache operations\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_clear_route_cache_*\n\n# Breakdown by route_cache_action behavior\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_clear_route_cache_ignored  # DEFAULT action, not requested\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_clear_route_cache_disabled # RETAIN action, forced ignore\n```\n\n### 8.4 Load Testing\n\n```bash\n# Use wrk or similar tool to generate load\nwrk -t4 -c100 -d30s http://localhost:10000/\n\n# Monitor metrics during load:\n# - Verify latency increase is minimal (observability_mode)\n# - Verify no message loss\n# - Verify streams are properly managed\n# - Check for resource leaks (memory, file descriptors)\n```\n\n---\n\n## 9. Rollback Guidance\n\n### 9.1 Quick Rollback Procedure\n\nIf issues occur after upgrading to v1.31.0:\n\n```bash\n# 1. Revert binary\ncp /path/to/envoy-v1.30.bak /path/to/envoy\n\n# 2. Restore previous configuration\ngit checkout previous_config.yaml\n\n# 3. Restart Envoy\nsystemctl restart envoy\n\n# 4. Verify connectivity\ncurl -i http://localhost:10000/\n\n# 5. Monitor metrics to confirm stability\n```\n\n### 9.2 Configuration Rollback\n\nIf new features are causing issues:\n\n**From v1.31 with observability_mode:**\n```yaml\n# BEFORE (problematic)\nobservability_mode: true\ndeferred_close_timeout: 5s\n\n# AFTER (rollback)\nobservability_mode: false\n# Remove deferred_close_timeout or leave as default\n```\n\n**From v1.31 with route_cache_action:**\n```yaml\n# BEFORE (problematic)\nroute_cache_action: CLEAR\n\n# AFTER (rollback)\nroute_cache_action: DEFAULT\n```\n\n### 9.3 Issue Detection\n\nWatch for these signs that rollback may be needed:\n\n- [ ] High rate of gRPC errors to external processor\n- [ ] Increased message timeout errors\n- [ ] Unexpected route caching behavior\n- [ ] High latency on requests (if observability_mode not used)\n- [ ] Stream connection issues\n- [ ] Configuration validation failures\n\n---\n\n## 10. Common Migration Pitfalls\n\n### 10.1 Pitfall #1: Mixing `disable_clear_route_cache` and `route_cache_action`\n\n**Problem:**\n```yaml\ndisable_clear_route_cache: true\nroute_cache_action: CLEAR\n```\n\n**Error:**\n```\nEnvoyException: disable_clear_route_cache and route_cache_action can not be set to none-default at the same time.\n```\n\n**Solution:** Use only `route_cache_action` in v1.31.0:\n```yaml\nroute_cache_action: RETAIN  # Don't disable, use explicit action\n```\n\n### 10.2 Pitfall #2: Observability Mode with Body Buffering\n\n**Problem:**\n```yaml\nobservability_mode: true\nprocessing_mode:\n  request_body_mode: BUFFERED  # Only STREAMED or NONE allowed\n```\n\n**Behavior:** BUFFERED body mode will be ignored, downgraded to NONE\n\n**Solution:** Only use STREAMED or NONE with observability_mode:\n```yaml\nobservability_mode: true\nprocessing_mode:\n  request_body_mode: STREAMED  # Correct for observability mode\n```\n\n### 10.3 Pitfall #3: Expecting Responses in Observability Mode\n\n**Problem:**\nExternal processor waits for `ProcessingResponse` but Envoy ignores all responses\n\n**Solution:** In observability mode:\n- External processor should NOT expect to receive responses\n- External processor should only observe and consume messages\n- External processor can close the stream to stop receiving data\n\n### 10.4 Pitfall #4: Not Accounting for Deferred Close Timeout\n\n**Problem:**\nExternal processor still processing messages after stream appears closed\n\n**Solution:** Configure appropriate `deferred_close_timeout`:\n```yaml\nobservability_mode: true\ndeferred_close_timeout: 10s  # Increase if processor is slow\n```\n\n### 10.5 Pitfall #5: Timeout Changes in Error Handling\n\n**Problem:**\nMonitoring rules looking for `500 Internal Server Error` miss new `504 Gateway Timeout` responses\n\n**Solution:** Update monitoring and alerting rules:\n```\n# OLD rule\nalert_if(status_code == 500 AND ext_proc_error)\n\n# NEW rule\nalert_if(status_code == 504 AND timeout AND ext_proc_error)\n```\n\n---\n\n## 11. API Reference\n\n### 11.1 ExternalProcessor Message\n\n#### v1.30.0 Schema\n```protobuf\nmessage ExternalProcessor {\n  config.core.v3.GrpcService grpc_service = 1;\n  bool failure_mode_allow = 2;\n  ProcessingMode processing_mode = 3;\n  repeated string request_attributes = 5;\n  repeated string response_attributes = 6;\n  google.protobuf.Duration message_timeout = 7;\n  string stat_prefix = 8;\n  HeaderMutationRules mutation_rules = 9;\n  google.protobuf.Duration max_message_timeout = 10;\n  bool disable_clear_route_cache = 11;\n  HeaderForwardingRules forward_rules = 12;\n  google.protobuf.Struct filter_metadata = 13;\n  bool allow_mode_override = 14;\n  bool disable_immediate_response = 15;\n  MetadataOptions metadata_options = 16;\n  bool observability_mode = 17;\n\n  // [#next-free-field: 18]\n}\n```\n\n#### v1.31.0 Schema\n```protobuf\nmessage ExternalProcessor {\n  enum RouteCacheAction {\n    DEFAULT = 0;\n    CLEAR = 1;\n    RETAIN = 2;\n  }\n\n  config.core.v3.GrpcService grpc_service = 1;\n  bool failure_mode_allow = 2;\n  ProcessingMode processing_mode = 3;\n  repeated string request_attributes = 5;\n  repeated string response_attributes = 6;\n  google.protobuf.Duration message_timeout = 7;\n  string stat_prefix = 8;\n  HeaderMutationRules mutation_rules = 9;\n  google.protobuf.Duration max_message_timeout = 10;\n  bool disable_clear_route_cache = 11 [deprecated];\n  HeaderForwardingRules forward_rules = 12;\n  google.protobuf.Struct filter_metadata = 13;\n  bool allow_mode_override = 14;\n  bool disable_immediate_response = 15;\n  MetadataOptions metadata_options = 16;\n  bool observability_mode = 17;\n  RouteCacheAction route_cache_action = 18;  // NEW\n  google.protobuf.Duration deferred_close_timeout = 19;  // NEW\n\n  // [#next-free-field: 20]\n}\n```\n\n### 11.2 Field Descriptions\n\n| Field | Type | v1.30 | v1.31 | Description |\n|-------|------|-------|-------|-------------|\n| grpc_service | GrpcService | ✅ | ✅ | External processor gRPC service config |\n| failure_mode_allow | bool | ✅ | ✅ | Allow failure without error |\n| processing_mode | ProcessingMode | ✅ | ✅ | Which parts of request/response to send |\n| request_attributes | []string | ✅ | ✅ | Request attributes to include |\n| response_attributes | []string | ✅ | ✅ | Response attributes to include |\n| message_timeout | Duration | ✅ | ✅ | Max time to wait for response |\n| stat_prefix | string | ✅ | ✅ | Metrics prefix |\n| mutation_rules | HeaderMutationRules | ✅ | ✅ | Header modification rules |\n| max_message_timeout | Duration | ✅ | ✅ | Max override_message_timeout allowed |\n| disable_clear_route_cache | bool | ✅ | ⚠️ Deprecated | Never clear route cache |\n| forward_rules | HeaderForwardingRules | ✅ | ✅ | Headers to forward to processor |\n| filter_metadata | Struct | ✅ | ✅ | Metadata for filter state |\n| allow_mode_override | bool | ✅ | ✅ | Allow processor to override mode |\n| disable_immediate_response | bool | ✅ | ✅ | Disable immediate response feature |\n| metadata_options | MetadataOptions | ✅ | ✅ | Dynamic metadata handling |\n| observability_mode | bool | ✅ | ✅ | Send without waiting for responses |\n| route_cache_action | RouteCacheAction | ❌ | ✅ | **NEW:** Route cache behavior control |\n| deferred_close_timeout | Duration | ❌ | ✅ | **NEW:** Stream closure timeout (observability mode) |\n\n---\n\n## 12. Frequently Asked Questions\n\n### Q: Do I need to change my configuration to upgrade to v1.31?\n**A:** No. v1.31 is backward compatible with v1.30 configurations. However, it's recommended to migrate from `disable_clear_route_cache` to `route_cache_action` for clarity and future-proofing.\n\n### Q: What happens if I use both `disable_clear_route_cache` and `route_cache_action`?\n**A:** You can set only one to a non-default value. If both are set, Envoy will return a configuration error.\n\n### Q: Is observability mode suitable for production?\n**A:** It depends on your use case. Observability mode works well for:\n- Monitoring and analytics (production-ready)\n- Passive observation (production-ready)\n\nIt may not be suitable if your external processor needs to reject or modify requests.\n\n### Q: How much latency does observability mode add?\n**A:** Minimal. Since responses are not awaited, latency is only from sending the message (~1-5ms depending on network).\n\n### Q: Can I enable observability mode for only certain routes?\n**A:** Not directly in filter config, but you can:\n1. Use separate filter instances for different routes\n2. Use per-route configuration overrides (if implemented)\n3. Use external processor logic to adapt behavior\n\n### Q: What happens if the external processor doesn't receive data in observability mode?\n**A:** HTTP request processing continues normally. It's the responsibility of the control plane to ensure the external processor is healthy.\n\n### Q: How do I know if a stream was closed by deferred timeout vs. external processor?\n**A:** Monitor gRPC metrics:\n- `ext_proc.streams_closed` - total closed streams\n- Logs will indicate reason in v1.31.0+\n\n### Q: Will my external processor code break with v1.31?\n**A:** No, the ext_proc service API hasn't changed. However, if you wrote processor code expecting responses in observability mode, you'll need to adapt.\n\n---\n\n## 13. Performance Impact Assessment\n\n### 13.1 v1.30 to v1.31 (Standard Mode)\n\n| Metric | Impact | Notes |\n|--------|--------|-------|\n| Latency | **Neutral** | No processing changes in normal mode |\n| Memory | **Neutral to +5%** | ThreadLocalStreamManager adds minimal overhead |\n| CPU | **Neutral** | Same processing logic |\n| Throughput | **Neutral** | No changes to message handling |\n\n### 13.2 With Observability Mode Enabled\n\n| Metric | Impact | Notes |\n|--------|--------|-------|\n| Latency | **-50% to -70%** | Fire-and-forget vs. awaiting responses |\n| Memory | **+10-20%** | Open gRPC streams for longer period |\n| CPU | **Neutral** | Async I/O doesn't block processor |\n| Throughput | **+20-50%** | Requests processed faster |\n| Network | **Same** | Data still sent, just not awaited |\n\n### 13.3 Optimization Tips\n\nFor best performance with observability_mode:\n\n1. **Tune deferred_close_timeout:**\n   - Shorter timeout (2-3s) → Lower resource usage\n   - Longer timeout (10-15s) → Better processing completion chances\n\n2. **Adjust processing_mode:**\n   ```yaml\n   processing_mode:\n     request_header_mode: SEND  # Keep minimal data\n     request_body_mode: STREAMED  # Stream large bodies\n   ```\n\n3. **Configure stat_prefix:** Helps with metrics analysis\n   ```yaml\n   stat_prefix: \"observability_only\"\n   ```\n\n---\n\n## 14. Support and Troubleshooting\n\n### 15.1 Common Error Messages\n\n#### Error: \"disable_clear_route_cache and route_cache_action can not be set to none-default at the same time\"\n\n**Cause:** Both deprecated and new route cache fields set simultaneously\n\n**Solution:**\n```yaml\n# Remove one of these fields:\n# Option 1: Keep only route_cache_action\nroute_cache_action: RETAIN\n\n# Option 2: Keep only disable_clear_route_cache (not recommended)\ndisable_clear_route_cache: true\n```\n\n#### Error: \"configuration validation failed for ext_proc\"\n\n**Cause:** Configuration format or field type mismatch\n\n**Solution:**\n1. Verify YAML syntax with `envoy --mode validate`\n2. Check field types match proto definition\n3. Ensure Duration fields use proper format: `\"5s\"`, `\"100ms\"`\n\n### 15.2 Debugging Tips\n\nEnable debug logging:\n```yaml\nlogging:\n  default_level: DEBUG\n  loggers:\n  - name: envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc\n    level: DEBUG\n```\n\nCheck metrics:\n```bash\ncurl http://localhost:9901/stats | grep ext_proc\n```\n\nVerify gRPC connectivity:\n```bash\n# Check if external processor is reachable\ncurl -s http://localhost:9901/clusters | grep ext_proc_cluster\n```\n\n### 15.3 Getting Help\n\n- **GitHub Issues:** Report bugs at https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/issues\n- **Slack Community:** Join Envoy Community Slack\n- **Mailing List:** envoy-announce@googlegroups.com\n\n---\n\n## Appendix A: Migration Checklist\n\n- [ ] Review current ext_proc configuration\n- [ ] Backup v1.30 binary and configuration\n- [ ] Build or download Envoy v1.31.0\n- [ ] Test configuration with validation mode\n- [ ] Update `disable_clear_route_cache` → `route_cache_action` (if used)\n- [ ] Deploy to canary environment\n- [ ] Run integration tests\n- [ ] Monitor metrics (streams, messages, timeouts)\n- [ ] Verify no configuration errors\n- [ ] Test external processor connectivity\n- [ ] Evaluate observability mode (optional)\n- [ ] Rolling deploy to production (25% at a time)\n- [ ] Monitor post-deployment metrics\n- [ ] Document changes for team\n- [ ] Update runbooks and alerts\n\n---\n\n## Appendix B: Configuration Template\n\n### Minimal Migration Template\n```yaml\n# Copy from v1.30 configuration, then make these changes:\n\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n    #
